---
src       : src/plfa/Quantitative.lagda
title     : "Quantitative: Counting Resources in Types"
layout    : page
permalink : /Quantitative/
---

In previous chapters, we introduced the lambda calculus, with [a formalisation based on named variables]({{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Lambda.md%}) and [an inherently-typed version]({{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/DeBruijn.md%}).  This chapter presents a refinement of those approaches, in which we not only care about the types of variables, but also about *how often they're used*.


# Introduction

Identity and constant function.

  - ``∅ , 1 ∙ "x" ⦂ A  ⊢ ` "x" ⦂ A``
  - ``∅ ⊢ (ƛ "x" ⇒ ` "x") ⦂ [ 1 ∙ A ]⊸ A``
  - ``∅ , 1 ∙ "x" ⦂ A , 0 ∙ "y" ⦂ B ⊢ ` "x" ⦂ A``
  - ``∅ ⊢ (ƛ "x" ⇒ ƛ "y" ⇒ ` "x") ⦂ [ 1 ∙ A ]⊸ [ 0 ∙ B ]⊸ A``

Some numbers.

  - ``∅ , 1 ∙ "z" ⦂ ℕ , 0 ∙ "s" ⦂ [ 1 ∙ ℕ ]⊸ ℕ ⊢ ` "z" ⦂ ℕ``
  - ``∅ , 1 ∙ "z" ⦂ ℕ , 1 ∙ "s" ⦂ [ 1 ∙ ℕ ]⊸ ℕ ⊢ (` "s" · ` "z") ⦂ ℕ``
  - ``∅ , 1 ∙ "z" ⦂ ℕ , ω ∙ "s" ⦂ [ 1 ∙ ℕ ]⊸ ℕ ⊢ (` "s" · (` "s" · ` "z")) ⦂ ℕ``


Words.

    data Mult : Set where
      0# : Mult
      1# : Mult
      ω# : Mult

Words.

    0# + π   =  π
    1# + 1#  =  ω#
    ω# + π   =  ω#

Words.

    0# * π   =  0#
    1# * π   =  π   if  π ≢ 0#
    ω# * π   =  ω#  if  π ≢ 0#

Words.

    0#    1#
      \  /
       ω#

# Contexts

Matrices.

See [this sidenote]({{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative/LinAlg.md%}).

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="Matrix"></a><a id="3189" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#3189" class="Function">Matrix</a> <a id="3196" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3198" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#2050" class="Datatype">Precontext</a> <a id="3209" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3211" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#2050" class="Datatype">Precontext</a> <a id="3222" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3224" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="3228" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#3189" class="Function">Matrix</a> <a id="3235" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#3235" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="3237" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#3237" class="Bound">δ</a> <a id="3239" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3241" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="3243" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3244" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#3244" class="Bound">A</a><a id="3245" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3247" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3249" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#3235" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="3251" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#2268" class="Datatype Operator">∋</a> <a id="3253" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#3244" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3255" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3257" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#2463" class="Datatype">Context</a> <a id="3265" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#3237" class="Bound">δ</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The identity matrix.

          "x"       "y"       "z"
    "x"  1 ∙ A  ,  0 ∙ B  ,  0 ∙ C
    "y"  0 ∙ A  ,  1 ∙ B  ,  0 ∙ C
    "z"  0 ∙ A  ,  0 ∙ B  ,  1 ∙ C

# Properties of vector operations

Unit scaling does nothing.

  <a id="4356" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4374" class="Function Operator">∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Scaling by a product is the composition of scalings.

Scaling the 0-vector gives the 0-vector.

Scaling by 0 gives the 0-vector.

Adding the 0-vector does nothing.

Vector addition is commutative.

Vector addition is associative.

Scaling by a sum gives the sum of the scalings.

Scaling a sum gives the sum of the scalings.

Adding a row of 0s to the end of the matrix and then multiplying by a vector produces a vector with a 0 at the bottom.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="⊛-zeroʳ"></a><a id="8787" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#8787" class="Function">⊛-zeroʳ</a> <a id="8795" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8797" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="8799" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8800" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#8800" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="8802" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#8802" class="Bound">δ</a><a id="8803" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8805" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8806" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#8806" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="8808" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8810" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#2463" class="Datatype">Context</a> <a id="8818" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#8800" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="8819" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8821" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8822" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#8822" class="Bound">Ξ</a> <a id="8824" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8826" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#3189" class="Function">Matrix</a> <a id="8833" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#8800" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="8835" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#8802" class="Bound">δ</a><a id="8836" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8838" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8839" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#8839" class="Bound">B</a><a id="8840" class="Symbol">}</a>

  <a id="8845" class="Comment">---------------------------------------------------</a>
  <a id="8899" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8901" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#8806" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="8903" href="{% endraw %}{{ Linear maps preserve scaling.

site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#10510" class="Bound">Ξ</a> <a id="11534" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Function.html#769" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="11536" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#2358" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">S_</a><a id="11538" class="Symbol">))</a>
  <a id="11543" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4374" class="Function Operator">∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Multiplying by a standard basis vector projects out the corresponding column of the matrix.

    <a id="12307" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#12052" class="Bound">Ξ</a> <a id="12309" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12310" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#2358" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">S</a> <a id="12312" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#12057" class="Bound">x</a><a id="12313" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="12317" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Binary.PropositionalEquality.html#4374" class="Function Operator">∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The standard basis vectors put together give the identity matrix.

# Simultaneous Substitution

Extend a matrix as the identity matrix -- add a zero to the end of every row, and add a new row with a 1 and the rest 0s.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="extm"></a><a id="15079" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#15079" class="Function">extm</a> <a id="15084" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15086" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="15088" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15089" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#15089" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="15091" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#15091" class="Bound">δ</a><a id="15092" class="Symbol">}</a>

  <a id="15097" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15099" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#3189" class="Function">Matrix</a> <a id="15106" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#15089" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="15108" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#15091" class="Bound">δ</a>
    <a id="15114" class="Comment">--------------------------------</a>
  <a id="15149" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15151" class="Symbol">(∀</a> <a id="15154" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15155" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#15155" class="Bound">B</a><a id="15156" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15158" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15160" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#3189" class="Function">Matrix</a> <a id="15167" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15168" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#15089" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="15170" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#2094" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="15172" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#15155" class="Bound">B</a><a id="15173" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15175" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15176" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#15091" class="Bound">δ</a> <a id="15178" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#2094" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="15180" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Quantitative.md %}{% raw %}#15155" class="Bound">B</a><a id="15181" class="Symbol">))</a>
